
#AVIALABLE CUSTOM LOCALISATION KEYS
#When adding new custom loc keys, add them to the appropriate category (or add a new one) and describe them. Name the strings "String_X" where x is its content.
# To not display anything, you can use 'localisation_key = ""'
# Please add one example sentence for each key.

#As this list grow organize with categories.
#Current loc keys in this file:
#Get[Race]Tolerance


### Races
#Ex: "High tolerance of Elven people"
defined_text = {
	name = GetElvenTolerance
	random = no

	text = {
		localisation_key = primary_tolerance_text
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = elven_administration
		}
	}	
	text = {
		localisation_key = high_tolerance_text
		trigger = {
			high_tolerance_elven_race_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = medium_tolerance_text
		trigger = {
			medium_tolerance_elven_race_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = low_tolerance_text
		trigger = {
			low_tolerance_elven_race_trigger = yes
		}
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetPolicyCentaur
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = PolicyExpulsion
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = racial_pop_centaur_expulsion
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = racial_focus_centaur }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = PolicyExpulsionFocus
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = racial_pop_centaur_expulsion
			has_country_modifier = racial_focus_centaur
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = PolicyPurge
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = racial_pop_centaur_purge
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = racial_focus_centaur }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = PolicyPurgeFocus
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = racial_pop_centaur_purge
			has_country_modifier = racial_focus_centaur
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = PolicyFocus
		trigger = { has_country_modifier = racial_focus_centaur }
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = PolicyNone
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

defined_text = {
	random = no
	name = GetMilAvailableCentaur
	text = {
		localisation_key = MilCurrentCentaur
		trigger = { is_variable_equal = { which = centaurRanking value = 1 } }
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = MilAvailableCentaur
		trigger = {
			mil_power = 200
			high_tolerance_centaur_race_trigger = yes
			OR = {
				check_variable = { which = nbcentaurDev value = 30 }
				has_country_modifier = centaur_administration
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = MilNotAvailableCentaur
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

		localisation_key = GetRacialMilTroll
		trigger = { has_country_modifier = troll_military }
	}
